## 3) Pronunciation templates expansion

For Greek you already saw:

-   `{{IPA|el|/ˈɣra.fo/}}`
    
-   `{{hyphenation|el|γρά|φω}}`
    

Those are stable on enwiktionary for many entries (including γράφω). (Example section source shows both.) [MediaWiki](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3AParsing_wikitext?utm_source=chatgpt.com)

Add audio while you’re here (optional; very common across Wiktionary):

```
TypeScript

function parsePronunciation(wt: string, lang: "el"): { IPA?: string; hyphenation?: string; audio?: string } {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  
  const ipaTpl \= tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "IPA" && (t.positional\[0\] \=== lang || t.named\["lang"\] \=== lang));  
  const hyphTpl \= tpls.find(t => (t.name \=== "hyphenation" || t.name \=== "hyph") && t.positional\[0\] \=== lang);  
  const audioTpl \= tpls.find(t => (t.name \=== "audio" || t.name \=== "audio-IPA") && (t.positional\[0\] \=== lang || t.named\["lang"\] \=== lang));  
  
  const IPA \= ipaTpl?.positional?.find(x => x.startsWith("/") && x.endsWith("/"));  
  const hyphenation \= hyphTpl ? hyphTpl.positional.slice(1).join("‧") : undefined;  
  
  // audio template shapes vary; keep minimal: grab the file name if present  
  const audio \= audioTpl?.positional?.find(x => /\\.(ogg|oga|wav|mp3)$/i.test(x));  
  
  return { IPA, hyphenation, audio };  
}
```

---

## 4) Template coverage expansion: verbs, nouns, adjectives, particles, numerals

### A) “head” template as a universal fallback

A lot of entries (especially function words) use:

-   `{{head|el|...}}`
    

Add a minimal `head` decoder:

```
TypeScript

type HeadInfo \= { pos?: string; tags?: string\[\] };  
  
function decodeHead(tpls: TemplateCall\[\], lang: string): HeadInfo | undefined {  
  const head \= tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "head" && t.positional\[0\] \=== lang);  
  if (!head) return undefined;  
  
  // head.positional: \[lang, pos, ...tags\]  
  const pos \= head.positional\[1\]?.trim();  
  const tags \= head.positional.slice(2).map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean);  
  return { pos, tags: tags.length ? tags : undefined };  
}
```

### B) Better `infl of` decoding (verbs + nominals + numerals)

Your running examples:

-   `{{infl of|el|γράφω||3s|spast}}` (έγραψε)
    
-   `{{infl of|el|γράφω||1s|spast}}` (έγραψα)
    

(These raw blocks are visible in page source on enwiktionary.) [MediaWiki](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3AParsing_wikitext?utm_source=chatgpt.com)

Implement a more systematic tag mapper:

```
TypeScript

type VerbFeatures \= {  
  person?: 1|2|3;  
  number?: "singular"|"plural";  
  tense?: "present"|"aorist"|"imperfect"|"future"|"unknown";  
  mood?: "indicative"|"subjunctive"|"imperative"|"unknown";  
  voice?: "active"|"middle"|"passive"|"unknown";  
};  
  
type NominalFeatures \= {  
  case?: "nominative"|"genitive"|"accusative"|"vocative"|"unknown";  
  number?: "singular"|"plural";  
  gender?: "m"|"f"|"n"|"unknown";  
};  
  
function decodeInflOfTags(tags: string\[\]): { verb?: VerbFeatures; nominal?: NominalFeatures; raw: string\[\] } {  
  const verb: VerbFeatures \= {};  
  const nominal: NominalFeatures \= {};  
  const raw \= tags.map(t => t.trim()).filter(Boolean);  
  
  for (const t0 of raw) {  
    const t \= t0.toLowerCase();  
  
    // Person+Number: 1s,2p,3s...  
    const pn \= /^(\[123\])(\[sp\])$/.exec(t);  
    if (pn) {  
      verb.person \= Number(pn\[1\]) as 1|2|3;  
      verb.number \= pn\[2\] \=== "s" ? "singular" : "plural";  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // Verb tense/mood/voice (extend as you observe more)  
    if (t \=== "spast") { verb.tense \= "aorist"; verb.mood \= "indicative"; verb.voice \= "active"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "pres")  { verb.tense \= "present"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "impf" || t \=== "imperfect") { verb.tense \= "imperfect"; verb.mood ??= "indicative"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "fut" || t \=== "future") { verb.tense \= "future"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "ind") verb.mood \= "indicative";  
    if (t \=== "subj") verb.mood \= "subjunctive";  
    if (t \=== "imp") verb.mood \= "imperative";  
    if (t \=== "act") verb.voice \= "active";  
    if (t \=== "mid") verb.voice \= "middle";  
    if (t \=== "pass") verb.voice \= "passive";  
  
    // Nominal tags (common in form pages across Wiktionary)  
    if (t \=== "nom") nominal.case \= "nominative";  
    if (t \=== "gen") nominal.case \= "genitive";  
    if (t \=== "acc") nominal.case \= "accusative";  
    if (t \=== "voc") nominal.case \= "vocative";  
    if (t \=== "sg" || t \=== "s") nominal.number \= "singular";  
    if (t \=== "pl" || t \=== "p") nominal.number \= "plural";  
    if (t \=== "m" || t \=== "f" || t \=== "n") nominal.gender \= t as any;  
  }  
  
  const hasVerb \= Object.keys(verb).length \> 0;  
  const hasNom \= Object.keys(nominal).length \> 0;  
  
  return { verb: hasVerb ? { ...verb, mood: verb.mood ?? "unknown", voice: verb.voice ?? "unknown", tense: verb.tense ?? "unknown" } : undefined,  
           nominal: hasNom ? { ...nominal, case: nominal.case ?? "unknown", gender: nominal.gender ?? "unknown" } : undefined,  
           raw };  
}
```

### C) Verb lemma mapper: expand around `el-verb` + `el-conjug-*`

Keep your current `el-verb` + `el-conjug-1st` logic, but generalize to `el-conjug-*`:

```
TypeScript

function findGreekConjugationTemplate(tpls: TemplateCall\[\]): TemplateCall | undefined {  
  // e.g. el-conjug-1st, el-conjug-2nd...  
  return tpls.find(t => t.name.startsWith("el-conjug-"));  
}
```

Also: don’t “guess” stems if absent; store what templates provide.

### D) Noun & adjective lemma templates: `el-noun`, `el-adj`

Add detection by template name; keep metadata minimal now (gender for nouns; comparative/superlative later).

```
TypeScript

function isElNounLemma(tpls: TemplateCall\[\]): boolean {  
  return !!tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "el-noun");  
}  
function isElAdjLemma(tpls: TemplateCall\[\]): boolean {  
  return !!tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "el-adj");  
}
```

### E) Particles / function words

Treat these as “function” PoS with `head` fallback:

```
TypeScript

function decodeFunctionWord(form: string, pron: any, head?: HeadInfo): GenericEntry {  
  return {  
    id: \`el:${form}\`,  
    language: "el",  
    type: "LEXEME",  
    form,  
    part\_of\_speech: head?.pos ? head.pos : "function",  
    pronunciation: pron?.IPA ? { IPA: pron.IPA } : undefined,  
    hyphenation: pron?.hyphenation,  
    definitions: \[\],  
  };  
}
```

### F) Numerals (minimal)

Many numeral entries are still “noun-like” in structure. For now:

-   if `posBlock.pos === "numeral"` or `head.pos === "numeral"` return `part_of_speech: "numeral"`
    
-   if it’s an `infl of`, treat nominal tags first; else lemma.
    

---

## 5) Wire it into the main fetch: etymology + multiple candidates

Here’s the upgraded `fetchWiktionary` skeleton (key parts only), using the new section tree layout:

```
TypeScript

export async function fetchWiktionary(queryTerm: string, opts: Wiktionary SDKOptions \= {}): Promise<EnrichedEntry\[\]> {  
  const edition \= opts.edition ?? "en";  
  const lang: "el" \= opts.lang ?? "el";  
  const followLemma \= opts.followLemma ?? true;  
  
  const sections \= await fetchSections(edition, queryTerm);  
  const tree \= buildSectionTree(sections.map(s => ({ index: s.index, line: s.line, level: Number(s.level) })));  
  
  const greekNode \= findLanguageNode(tree, "Greek");  
  if (!greekNode) return \[\];  
  
  const layout \= extractGreekLayout(greekNode);  
  
  const pronWT \= layout.pronunciationSection  
    ? await fetchSectionWikitext(edition, queryTerm, layout.pronunciationSection)  
    : "";  
  const pron \= parsePronunciation(pronWT, lang);  
  
  const candidates: EnrichedEntry\[\] \= \[\];  
  
  for (const block of layout.posBlocks) {  
    // pos heading can be "verb", "noun", "adjective", "pronoun", etc.  
    const pos \= block.pos;  
  
    // optional filter by hint  
    if (opts.posHint && pos !== opts.posHint) {  
      // allow synonyms: "participle" often appears under adjective/verb; keep minimal  
    }  
  
    const wt \= await fetchSectionWikitext(edition, queryTerm, block.sectionIndex);  
    const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
    const head \= decodeHead(tpls, lang);  
  
    // INFLECTED\_FORM?  
    const infl \= tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "infl of" && t.positional\[0\] \=== lang);  
    if (infl) {  
      const lemma \= infl.positional\[1\];  
      const tags \= infl.positional.slice(2).filter(Boolean);  
      const decoded \= decodeInflOfTags(tags);  
  
      if (pos \=== "verb" || head?.pos \=== "verb") {  
        candidates.push({  
          id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, "verb"),  
          language: lang,  
          type: "INFLECTED\_FORM",  
          form: queryTerm,  
          part\_of\_speech: "verb",  
          pronunciation: pron.IPA ? { IPA: pron.IPA } : undefined,  
          hyphenation: pron.hyphenation,  
          lemma,  
          inflection: decoded.verb ? {  
            person: decoded.verb.person,  
            number: decoded.verb.number,  
            tense: decoded.verb.tense \=== "aorist" ? "simple\_past" : decoded.verb.tense,  
            mood: decoded.verb.mood,  
            voice: decoded.verb.voice,  
          } : undefined,  
        });  
        continue;  
      }  
  
      if (pos \=== "noun" || head?.pos \=== "noun" || pos \=== "numeral" || head?.pos \=== "numeral") {  
        candidates.push({  
          id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, pos),  
          language: lang,  
          type: "INFLECTED\_FORM",  
          form: queryTerm,  
          part\_of\_speech: pos \=== "numeral" ? "numeral" : "noun",  
          pronunciation: pron.IPA ? { IPA: pron.IPA } : undefined,  
          hyphenation: pron.hyphenation,  
          lemma,  
          inflection: decoded.nominal,  
        } as any);  
        continue;  
      }  
  
      if (pos \=== "adjective" || head?.pos \=== "adjective" || pos \=== "participle") {  
        candidates.push({  
          id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, "adjective"),  
          language: lang,  
          type: "INFLECTED\_FORM",  
          form: queryTerm,  
          part\_of\_speech: "adjective",  
          pronunciation: pron.IPA ? { IPA: pron.IPA } : undefined,  
          hyphenation: pron.hyphenation,  
          lemma,  
          inflection: decoded.nominal,  
        } as any);  
        continue;  
      }  
  
      // fallback inflected  
      candidates.push(mapGenericInflected(queryTerm, lang, pos, infl, pron));  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // LEMMA decoders  
    if (pos \=== "verb") {  
      candidates.push({  
        ...mapVerbLemma(queryTerm, lang, wt, pron),  
        id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, "verb"),  
      });  
      continue;  
    }  
    if (pos \=== "noun") {  
      candidates.push({  
        ...mapNounLemma(queryTerm, lang, wt, pron),  
        id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, "noun"),  
      });  
      continue;  
    }  
    if (pos \=== "adjective") {  
      candidates.push({  
        ...mapAdjectiveLemma(queryTerm, lang, wt, pron),  
        id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, "adjective"),  
      });  
      continue;  
    }  
    if (pos \=== "numeral" || head?.pos \=== "numeral") {  
      candidates.push({  
        ...mapGenericLemma(queryTerm, lang, "numeral", wt, pron),  
        id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, "numeral"),  
      });  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // function words / particles etc.  
    candidates.push({  
      ...decodeFunctionWord(queryTerm, pron, head),  
      id: mkId(queryTerm, block.etymology, head?.pos ?? pos),  
    });  
  }  
  
  // Follow lemma merge (your two-step strategy)  
  const merged \= followLemma  
    ? await Promise.all(candidates.map(async (c) => {  
        if (c.type !== "INFLECTED\_FORM") return c;  
        const lemma \= (c as any).lemma as string | undefined;  
        if (!lemma) return c;  
        const lemmaEntries \= await fetchWiktionary(lemma, { ...opts, followLemma: false });  
        return mergeInflectedWithLemma(c, lemmaEntries) as EnrichedEntry;  
      }))  
    : candidates;  
  
  // Optional Wikidata enrichment (works for lemma and inflected forms alike)  
  if (opts.enrich?.includeWikidata) {  
    return await Promise.all(merged.map(e => enrichWithWikidata(e, opts.enrich!, edition)));  
  }  
  
  return merged;  
}  
  
function mkId(form: string, etymology: string | undefined, pos: string): string {  
  const et \= etymology ? \`#${etymology.replace(/\\s+/g, "")}\` : "";  
  return \`el:${form}${et}#${pos}\`;  
}
```

That’s the homonymy story: **you keep multiple candidates** rather than collapsing them.

---

## 6) New feature: attach Wikidata QID → Wikipedia sitelinks → image

### Step 1: get the QID from the Wiktionary page via `pageprops.wikibase_item`

MediaWiki explicitly documents the `wikibase_item` page property approach. [MediaWiki+1](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3APresenting_Wikidata_knowledge?utm_source=chatgpt.com)

```
TypeScript

type MWQueryPagePropsResponse \= {  
  query?: {  
    pages?: Record<string, {  
      title: string;  
      pageprops?: { wikibase\_item?: string };  
    }>;  
  };  
  error?: { code: string; info: string };  
};  
  
async function fetchWikibaseItemFromWiktionaryTitle(edition: "en", title: string): Promise<string | null\> {  
  const url \= new URL(apiBase(edition));  
  url.searchParams.set("action", "query");  
  url.searchParams.set("prop", "pageprops");  
  url.searchParams.set("ppprop", "wikibase\_item");  
  url.searchParams.set("titles", title);  
  url.searchParams.set("format", "json");  
  url.searchParams.set("formatversion", "2");  
  url.searchParams.set("origin", "\*");  
  
  const res \= await fetch(url.toString());  
  if (!res.ok) return null;  
  
  const json \= (await res.json()) as MWQueryPagePropsResponse;  
  if (json.error) return null;  
  
  const pages \= json.query?.pages;  
  if (!pages) return null;  
  
  const first \= Object.values(pages)\[0\];  
  return first?.pageprops?.wikibase\_item ?? null;  
}
```

### Step 2: fetch Wikidata entity (labels, sitelinks, P18 image)

Wikibase API is documented and stable; you’ll call `wbgetentities`. [MediaWiki](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Wikibase/API?utm_source=chatgpt.com)  
Image is property `P18`. [wikidata.org](https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Property%3AP18?utm_source=chatgpt.com)

```
TypeScript

type WikidataEntityResponse \= {  
  entities?: Record<string, {  
    id: string;  
    labels?: Record<string, { language: string; value: string }>;  
    descriptions?: Record<string, { language: string; value: string }>;  
    sitelinks?: Record<string, { site: string; title: string; url?: string }>;  
    claims?: Record<string, Array<{  
      mainsnak?: {  
        datavalue?: { value?: any };  
      };  
    }>>;  
  }>;  
};  
  
async function fetchWikidataEntity(qid: string, languages: string\[\]): Promise<WikidataEnrichment | null\> {  
  const url \= new URL("https://www.wikidata.org/w/api.php");  
  url.searchParams.set("action", "wbgetentities");  
  url.searchParams.set("ids", qid);  
  url.searchParams.set("props", "labels|descriptions|sitelinks|claims");  
  url.searchParams.set("languages", languages.join("|"));  
  url.searchParams.set("format", "json");  
  url.searchParams.set("origin", "\*");  
  
  const res \= await fetch(url.toString());  
  if (!res.ok) return null;  
  
  const json \= (await res.json()) as WikidataEntityResponse;  
  const ent \= json.entities?.\[qid\];  
  if (!ent) return null;  
  
  const labels: Record<string, string\> \= {};  
  const descriptions: Record<string, string\> \= {};  
  
  for (const \[k, v\] of Object.entries(ent.labels ?? {})) labels\[k\] \= v.value;  
  for (const \[k, v\] of Object.entries(ent.descriptions ?? {})) descriptions\[k\] \= v.value;  
  
  // P18 (image) returns a Commons filename string in the claim value.  
  const images \= extractP18Images(ent.claims ?? {});  
  const sitelinks \= ent.sitelinks ?? {};  
  
  return {  
    qid,  
    labels: Object.keys(labels).length ? labels : undefined,  
    descriptions: Object.keys(descriptions).length ? descriptions : undefined,  
    sitelinks: Object.keys(sitelinks).length ? sitelinks : undefined,  
    images: images.length ? images : undefined,  
  };  
}  
  
function extractP18Images(claims: Record<string, any\[\]>): Array<{ filename: string; commonsUrl: string }> {  
  const p18 \= claims\["P18"\];  
  if (!Array.isArray(p18)) return \[\];  
  
  const files: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  for (const c of p18) {  
    const v \= c?.mainsnak?.datavalue?.value;  
    if (typeof v \=== "string" && v.length) files.push(v);  
  }  
  
  // de-dupe  
  const seen \= new Set<string\>();  
  const out: Array<{ filename: string; commonsUrl: string }> \= \[\];  
  for (const f of files) {  
    if (seen.has(f)) continue;  
    seen.add(f);  
    out.push({  
      filename: f,  
      commonsUrl: commonsFilePathUrl(f),  
    });  
  }  
  return out;  
}
```

### Step 3: build image URLs from Commons filenames

Commons explicitly documents that you can hotlink images via `Special:FilePath` / `Special:Redirect/file` (and you can request a width). [Wikimedia Commons+1](https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Commons%3AReusing_content_outside_Wikimedia/technical?utm_source=chatgpt.com)

```
TypeScript

function commonsFilePathUrl(filename: string, widthPx?: number): string {  
  // Use Special:Redirect/file because width is straightforward.  
  // filename should be the raw "Example.jpg" without "File:".  
  const base \= "https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/index.php";  
  const u \= new URL(base);  
  u.searchParams.set("title", \`Special:Redirect/file/${filename}\`);  
  if (widthPx && widthPx \> 0) u.searchParams.set("width", String(widthPx));  
  return u.toString();  
}
```

### Step 4: attach enrichment to entries

```
TypeScript

async function enrichWithWikidata(  
  entry: EnrichedEntry,  
  enrich: WikiEnrichmentOptions,  
  edition: "en"  
): Promise<EnrichedEntry\> {  
  const languages \= enrich.wikidataLanguages ?? \["en", "el"\];  
  const qid \= await fetchWikibaseItemFromWiktionaryTitle(edition, entry.form);  
  if (!qid) return entry;  
  
  const wd \= await fetchWikidataEntity(qid, languages);  
  if (!wd) return entry;  
  
  // Add thumb urls (optional)  
  const width \= enrich.imageWidth;  
  if (width && wd.images?.length) {  
    wd.images \= wd.images.map(img => ({  
      ...img,  
      thumbUrl: commonsFilePathUrl(img.filename, width),  
    }));  
  }  
  
  // Add Wikipedia URL convenience (optional; many sitelinks already include url, but not always)  
  // If missing, you can construct: https://{lang}.wikipedia.org/wiki/{title}  
  if (wd.sitelinks) {  
    for (const s of Object.values(wd.sitelinks)) {  
      if (!s.url && s.site.endsWith("wiki")) {  
        // example site keys: "enwiki", "elwiki"  
        const lang \= s.site.replace("wiki", "");  
        s.url \= \`https://${lang}.wikipedia.org/wiki/${encodeURIComponent(s.title.replace(/ /g, "\_"))}\`;  
      }  
    }  
  }  
  
  return { ...entry, wikidata: wd };  
}
```

That gives you exactly your “spanakopita” use case: **Wiktionary lexicography + Wikidata image + Wikipedia sitelinks**.

---

## 7) Practical notes (what will still bite you)

-   **Not every Wiktionary entry has a Wikidata item** (so `wikibase_item` might be absent).
    
-   **Inflected-form pages** often don’t have their own QID; you’ll likely want to enrich using the **lemma** QID (your merge step already makes that easy).
    
-   **Images**: `P18` is great for “spanakopita”; not all lexical items have a good P18 image. For people/places it’s usually decent; for function words it won’t exist.
    

---

    -   detect mediopassive lemmas (`-ομαι`) vs active (`-ω`)
        
3.  **Richer sense/translation extraction**:
    
    -   definitions are currently lines starting with `#`; you’ll want to parse sense qualifiers `{{q|...}}`, examples `{{ux|...}}`, and translation blocks.

## One Clarification Before I Generate the Full Implementation

There’s one subtle ambiguity I need you to confirm before I finalize the code and example outputs:

**When enriching with Wikidata images/sitelinks, for inflected forms should we:**

1.  **Always use the lemma’s Wikidata entity**, even if the form’s own page has a separate QID (rare but possible), *or*
    
2.  **Prefer the inflected form’s own QID if present**, and only if absent, then fallback to the lemma’s QID
    

**Choose A or B:**

-   **A)** lemma-centric enrichment  
    Ex: *έγραψε* → use *γράφω*’s Wikidata item
    
-   **B)** form-centric enrichment  
    Ex: if *έγραψε* itself has a Wikidata item, use that; otherwise fallback to lemma
    

Reply simply with **“A” or “B”**, and I’ll proceed to generate the full TypeScript implementation and real example output with that assumption applied.

You: 

I choose A. We should only enrich lemma-type entries, so be lemma-centric.

ChatGPT: 

Nagedacht gedurende 33s

Below is a **next-iteration, end-to-end TypeScript module** that implements what you requested:

-   **English Wiktionary only** (as primary source)
    
-   **Language section + etymology/homonymy aware parsing**
    
-   **Fetch Wikitext by section** (`action=parse&prop=sections` + `action=parse&prop=wikitext&section=N`) [MediaWiki](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3AParsing_wikitext?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
    
-   **Minimal `{{…}}` template parser** (nesting-safe)
    
-   **Coverage expansion**:
    
    -   verbs: `infl of`, `el-verb`, `el-conjug-*`, `ux`
        
    -   nouns: `infl of`, `el-noun`
        
    -   adjectives / participles: `infl of`, `el-adj`
        
    -   numerals + function words: `head`
        
    -   pronunciation: `IPA`, `hyphenation`, (optional `audio`)
        
-   **Better inflection decoding** (verb + nominal tags)
    
-   **Homonymy handling**: returns *multiple candidates* split by **Etymology 1/2/…** (when present)
    
-   **Lemma-centric Wikidata enrichment** (only `type: "LEXEME"`):
    
    -   QID via `pageprops` → `wikibase_item` [MediaWiki+1](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3APresenting_Wikidata_knowledge?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
        
    -   entity via `wbgetentities` [MediaWiki](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3APresenting_Wikidata_knowledge?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
        
    -   images via `P18` [MediaWiki](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3APresenting_Wikidata_knowledge?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
        
    -   Commons thumbnail via redirect URL method [MediaWiki](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/API%3APresenting_Wikidata_knowledge?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
        

> Design choice matching your “A”: **inflected forms are not enriched**; only lemma entries get `wikidata`. Inflected entries point to lemma via `lemma.id` and you can render media from the lemma object.

---

```
TypeScript

/\* wikiFetch.ts  
 \*  
 \* English Wiktionary (Greek extraction) + lemma-centric Wikidata enrichment.  
 \*  
 \* Requires: global fetch (Node 18+ or undici/polyfill)  
 \*/  
  
export type WikiLang \= "el";  
  
export type Pos \=  
  | "verb"  
  | "noun"  
  | "adjective"  
  | "participle"  
  | "adverb"  
  | "numeral"  
  | "article"  
  | "pronoun"  
  | "preposition"  
  | "conjunction"  
  | "particle"  
  | "interjection"  
  | "function"  
  | "unknown";  
  
export type EntryType \= "LEXEME" | "INFLECTED\_FORM";  
  
export type Wiktionary SDKOptions \= {  
  lang?: WikiLang;                  // default "el"  
  posHint?: Pos;                    // optional filter hint  
  followLemma?: boolean;            // default true: if query is inflected, fetch lemma and include lemma entry  
  includeLemmaEntry?: boolean;      // default true: return lemma entry in results alongside inflected  
  timeoutMs?: number;               // default 15000  
  
  enrich?: WikiEnrichmentOptions;   // Wikidata/Wikipedia/media  
};  
  
export type WikiEnrichmentOptions \= {  
  includeWikidata?: boolean;        // default false  
  wikidataLanguages?: string\[\];     // default \["en","el"\]  
  imageWidth?: number;             // e.g. 320  
};  
  
export type Pronunciation \= {  
  IPA?: string;  
  hyphenation?: string;  
  audio?: string; // filename if any  
};  
  
export type UsageExample \= {  
  el?: string;  
  en?: string;  
  note?: string;  
};  
  
export type LemmaRef \= {  
  id: string;       // e.g. "el:γράφω#verb"  
  form: string;     // "γράφω"  
  pos?: Pos;  
};  
  
export type WikidataEnrichment \= {  
  qid: string;  
  labels?: Record<string, string\>;  
  descriptions?: Record<string, string\>;  
  sitelinks?: Record<string, { site: string; title: string; url?: string }>;  
  images?: Array<{ filename: string; commonsUrl: string; thumbUrl?: string }>;  
};  
  
export type BaseEntry \= {  
  id: string;                // stable within our extractor  
  language: WikiLang;  
  type: EntryType;  
  pos: Pos;  
  form: string;  
  
  etymology?: string;        // "Etymology 1" etc, if applicable  
  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation;  
  
  // Definitions (English gloss lines, as best-effort)  
  senses?: Array<{  
    gloss?: string;          // stripped from wikitext line(s)  
    usage?: UsageExample\[\];  // from {{ux|el|...|t=...}}  
  }>;  
  
  // Debug/tracing (optional; useful while expanding coverage)  
  \_debug?: {  
    wiktionary: {  
      domain: string;  
      pageTitle: string;  
      sectionIndex?: string;  
      sectionHeading?: string;  
    };  
    templates?: Array<{ name: string; raw: string }>;  
    unknownTemplates?: string\[\];  
  };  
};  
  
export type VerbLexeme \= BaseEntry & {  
  type: "LEXEME";  
  pos: "verb";  
  class?: string;                // e.g. "verb.act.ω" (heuristic)  
  voiceType?: "active" | "mediopassive" | "unknown";  
  
  morphology?: {  
    presentStem?: string;  
    aoristStem?: string;  
    augment?: string;  
    ending?: string;  
  };  
  
  paradigm?: {  
    present\_1sg?: string;  
    aorist\_1sg?: string;  
    imperfect\_3sg?: string;  
    passive\_present?: string;  
    passive\_aorist?: string;  
  };  
  
  derivations?: string\[\];        // from {{l|el|...}} in related/derived sections (best-effort)  
  
  wikidata?: WikidataEnrichment; // lemma-centric enrichment only  
};  
  
export type VerbInflected \= BaseEntry & {  
  type: "INFLECTED\_FORM";  
  pos: "verb";  
  lemma: LemmaRef;  
  
  inflection?: Partial<{  
    person: 1 | 2 | 3;  
    number: "singular" | "plural";  
    tense: "present" | "aorist" | "imperfect" | "future" | "unknown";  
    mood: "indicative" | "subjunctive" | "imperative" | "unknown";  
    voice: "active" | "middle" | "passive" | "unknown";  
  }>;  
};  
  
export type NounLexeme \= BaseEntry & {  
  type: "LEXEME";  
  pos: "noun";  
  gender?: "m" | "f" | "n" | "unknown";  
  wikidata?: WikidataEnrichment;  
};  
  
export type NounInflected \= BaseEntry & {  
  type: "INFLECTED\_FORM";  
  pos: "noun";  
  lemma: LemmaRef;  
  inflection?: Partial<{  
    case: "nominative" | "genitive" | "accusative" | "vocative" | "unknown";  
    number: "singular" | "plural";  
    gender: "m" | "f" | "n" | "unknown";  
  }>;  
};  
  
export type AdjectiveLexeme \= BaseEntry & {  
  type: "LEXEME";  
  pos: "adjective";  
  wikidata?: WikidataEnrichment;  
};  
  
export type AdjectiveInflected \= BaseEntry & {  
  type: "INFLECTED\_FORM";  
  pos: "adjective" | "participle";  
  lemma: LemmaRef;  
  inflection?: Partial<{  
    case: "nominative" | "genitive" | "accusative" | "vocative" | "unknown";  
    number: "singular" | "plural";  
    gender: "m" | "f" | "n" | "unknown";  
  }>;  
};  
  
export type GenericLexeme \= BaseEntry & {  
  type: "LEXEME";  
  pos:  
    | "numeral"  
    | "adverb"  
    | "article"  
    | "pronoun"  
    | "preposition"  
    | "conjunction"  
    | "particle"  
    | "interjection"  
    | "function"  
    | "unknown";  
  wikidata?: WikidataEnrichment;  
};  
  
export type Entry \=  
  | VerbLexeme  
  | VerbInflected  
  | NounLexeme  
  | NounInflected  
  | AdjectiveLexeme  
  | AdjectiveInflected  
  | GenericLexeme;  
  
export type FetchResult \= {  
  query: { term: string; lang: WikiLang; posHint?: Pos };  
  entries: Entry\[\];  
  warnings: string\[\];  
};  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* MediaWiki / Wiktionary clients  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
const WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN \= "en.wiktionary.org";  
const WIKTIONARY\_API \= \`https://${WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN}/w/api.php\`;  
  
async function fetchJsonWithTimeout<T\>(url: string, timeoutMs: number): Promise<T\> {  
  const controller \= new AbortController();  
  const t \= setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs);  
  try {  
    const res \= await fetch(url, { signal: controller.signal });  
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(\`HTTP ${res.status} ${res.statusText}\`);  
    return (await res.json()) as T;  
  } finally {  
    clearTimeout(t);  
  }  
}  
  
type MWParseSectionsResponse \= {  
  parse?: {  
    title?: string;  
    pageid?: number;  
    sections?: Array<{  
      index: string;  
      line: string;  
      level: string;  
    }>;  
  };  
  error?: { code: string; info: string };  
};  
  
type MWParseWikitextResponse \= {  
  parse?: {  
    title?: string;  
    wikitext?: string; // formatversion=2 gives string  
  };  
  error?: { code: string; info: string };  
};  
  
async function mwParseSections(title: string, timeoutMs: number): Promise<MWParseSectionsResponse\> {  
  const u \= new URL(WIKTIONARY\_API);  
  u.searchParams.set("action", "parse");  
  u.searchParams.set("page", title);  
  u.searchParams.set("prop", "sections");  
  u.searchParams.set("format", "json");  
  u.searchParams.set("formatversion", "2");  
  u.searchParams.set("origin", "\*");  
  return await fetchJsonWithTimeout<MWParseSectionsResponse\>(u.toString(), timeoutMs);  
}  
  
async function mwParseWikitext(title: string, sectionIndex: string, timeoutMs: number): Promise<MWParseWikitextResponse\> {  
  const u \= new URL(WIKTIONARY\_API);  
  u.searchParams.set("action", "parse");  
  u.searchParams.set("page", title);  
  u.searchParams.set("prop", "wikitext");  
  u.searchParams.set("section", sectionIndex);  
  u.searchParams.set("format", "json");  
  u.searchParams.set("formatversion", "2");  
  u.searchParams.set("origin", "\*");  
  return await fetchJsonWithTimeout<MWParseWikitextResponse\>(u.toString(), timeoutMs);  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* Wikidata enrichment (lemma-centric)  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
type MWQueryPagePropsResponse \= {  
  query?: {  
    pages?: Array<{  
      title: string;  
      pageid: number;  
      pageprops?: { wikibase\_item?: string };  
    }>;  
  };  
  error?: { code: string; info: string };  
};  
  
async function mwGetWikibaseItemFromPage(title: string, timeoutMs: number): Promise<string | null\> {  
  const u \= new URL(WIKTIONARY\_API);  
  u.searchParams.set("action", "query");  
  u.searchParams.set("prop", "pageprops");  
  u.searchParams.set("ppprop", "wikibase\_item");  
  u.searchParams.set("titles", title);  
  u.searchParams.set("format", "json");  
  u.searchParams.set("formatversion", "2");  
  u.searchParams.set("origin", "\*");  
  const json \= await fetchJsonWithTimeout<MWQueryPagePropsResponse\>(u.toString(), timeoutMs);  
  if (json.error) return null;  
  const page \= json.query?.pages?.\[0\];  
  return page?.pageprops?.wikibase\_item ?? null;  
}  
  
type WikidataEntityResponse \= {  
  entities?: Record<  
    string,  
    {  
      id: string;  
      labels?: Record<string, { language: string; value: string }>;  
      descriptions?: Record<string, { language: string; value: string }>;  
      sitelinks?: Record<string, { site: string; title: string; url?: string }>;  
      claims?: Record<  
        string,  
        Array<{  
          mainsnak?: { datavalue?: { value?: any } };  
        }>  
      >;  
    }  
  >;  
  error?: { code: string; info: string };  
};  
  
async function wdGetEntity(qid: string, languages: string\[\], timeoutMs: number): Promise<WikidataEnrichment | null\> {  
  const u \= new URL("https://www.wikidata.org/w/api.php");  
  u.searchParams.set("action", "wbgetentities");  
  u.searchParams.set("ids", qid);  
  u.searchParams.set("props", "labels|descriptions|sitelinks|claims");  
  u.searchParams.set("languages", languages.join("|"));  
  u.searchParams.set("format", "json");  
  u.searchParams.set("formatversion", "2");  
  u.searchParams.set("origin", "\*");  
  
  const json \= await fetchJsonWithTimeout<WikidataEntityResponse\>(u.toString(), timeoutMs);  
  if (json.error) return null;  
  
  const ent \= json.entities?.\[qid\];  
  if (!ent) return null;  
  
  const labels: Record<string, string\> \= {};  
  const descriptions: Record<string, string\> \= {};  
  
  for (const \[k, v\] of Object.entries(ent.labels ?? {})) labels\[k\] \= v.value;  
  for (const \[k, v\] of Object.entries(ent.descriptions ?? {})) descriptions\[k\] \= v.value;  
  
  const sitelinks \= ent.sitelinks ?? {};  
  const images \= extractP18(ent.claims ?? {});  
  
  return {  
    qid,  
    labels: Object.keys(labels).length ? labels : undefined,  
    descriptions: Object.keys(descriptions).length ? descriptions : undefined,  
    sitelinks: Object.keys(sitelinks).length ? sitelinks : undefined,  
    images: images.length ? images : undefined,  
  };  
}  
  
function extractP18(  
  claims: Record<string, Array<{ mainsnak?: { datavalue?: { value?: any } } }>>  
): Array<{ filename: string; commonsUrl: string; thumbUrl?: string }> {  
  const p18 \= claims\["P18"\];  
  if (!Array.isArray(p18)) return \[\];  
  
  const files: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  for (const c of p18) {  
    const v \= c?.mainsnak?.datavalue?.value;  
    if (typeof v \=== "string" && v) files.push(v);  
  }  
  
  const seen \= new Set<string\>();  
  const out: Array<{ filename: string; commonsUrl: string; thumbUrl?: string }> \= \[\];  
  for (const f of files) {  
    if (seen.has(f)) continue;  
    seen.add(f);  
    out.push({ filename: f, commonsUrl: commonsRedirectUrl(f) });  
  }  
  return out;  
}  
  
function commonsRedirectUrl(filename: string, widthPx?: number): string {  
  // Commons redirect endpoint supports width param.  
  const u \= new URL("https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/index.php");  
  u.searchParams.set("title", \`Special:Redirect/file/${filename}\`);  
  if (widthPx && widthPx \> 0) u.searchParams.set("width", String(widthPx));  
  return u.toString();  
}  
  
function ensureWikipediaUrls(sitelinks: WikidataEnrichment\["sitelinks"\]): void {  
  if (!sitelinks) return;  
  for (const s of Object.values(sitelinks)) {  
    if (s.url) continue;  
    if (!s.site.endsWith("wiki")) continue; // e.g. enwiki, elwiki  
    const lang \= s.site.replace(/wiki$/, "");  
    s.url \= \`https://${lang}.wikipedia.org/wiki/${encodeURIComponent(s.title.replace(/ /g, "\_"))}\`;  
  }  
}  
  
async function enrichLemmaOnly(  
  lemmaEntry: Entry,  
  title: string,  
  enrich: WikiEnrichmentOptions,  
  timeoutMs: number  
): Promise<Entry\> {  
  if (lemmaEntry.type !== "LEXEME") return lemmaEntry;  
  if (!enrich.includeWikidata) return lemmaEntry;  
  
  const qid \= await mwGetWikibaseItemFromPage(title, timeoutMs);  
  if (!qid) return lemmaEntry;  
  
  const languages \= enrich.wikidataLanguages ?? \["en", "el"\];  
  const wd \= await wdGetEntity(qid, languages, timeoutMs);  
  if (!wd) return lemmaEntry;  
  
  ensureWikipediaUrls(wd.sitelinks);  
  
  const w \= enrich.imageWidth;  
  if (w && wd.images?.length) {  
    wd.images \= wd.images.map(img => ({ ...img, thumbUrl: commonsRedirectUrl(img.filename, w) }));  
  }  
  
  return { ...lemmaEntry, wikidata: wd } as Entry;  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* Section tree and Greek layout (homonymy-aware)  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
type MWSection \= { index: string; line: string; level: number };  
type SectionNode \= MWSection & { children: SectionNode\[\] };  
  
function buildSectionTree(sections: MWSection\[\]): SectionNode\[\] {  
  const root: SectionNode\[\] \= \[\];  
  const stack: SectionNode\[\] \= \[\];  
  for (const s of sections) {  
    const node: SectionNode \= { ...s, children: \[\] };  
    while (stack.length && stack\[stack.length \- 1\].level \>= node.level) stack.pop();  
    if (!stack.length) root.push(node);  
    else stack\[stack.length \- 1\].children.push(node);  
    stack.push(node);  
  }  
  return root;  
}  
  
function findLanguageNode(tree: SectionNode\[\], languageHeading: string): SectionNode | undefined {  
  return tree.find(n => n.level \=== 2 && n.line \=== languageHeading);  
}  
  
function isEtymologyHeading(line: string): boolean {  
  return /^Etymology\\s+\\d+$/i.test(line.trim());  
}  
  
type PosBlock \= {  
  etymology?: string;  
  posHeading: string;        // raw heading, normalized later  
  sectionIndex: string;  
  sectionHeading: string;    // for debug  
};  
  
type GreekLayout \= {  
  pronunciationSection?: string;  
  blocks: PosBlock\[\];  
};  
  
function extractGreekLayout(greekNode: SectionNode): GreekLayout {  
  const layout: GreekLayout \= { blocks: \[\] };  
  
  for (const child of greekNode.children) {  
    if (child.level !== 3) continue;  
  
    if (child.line \=== "Pronunciation") {  
      layout.pronunciationSection \= child.index;  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    if (isEtymologyHeading(child.line)) {  
      const et \= child.line;  
      for (const posNode of child.children) {  
        if (posNode.level \=== 4) {  
          layout.blocks.push({  
            etymology: et,  
            posHeading: posNode.line,  
            sectionIndex: posNode.index,  
            sectionHeading: posNode.line,  
          });  
        }  
      }  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // No etymology: POS at level 3  
    layout.blocks.push({  
      posHeading: child.line,  
      sectionIndex: child.index,  
      sectionHeading: child.line,  
    });  
  }  
  
  return layout;  
}  
  
function headingToPos(h: string): Pos {  
  const x \= h.trim().toLowerCase();  
  if (x \=== "verb") return "verb";  
  if (x \=== "noun") return "noun";  
  if (x \=== "adjective") return "adjective";  
  if (x \=== "participle") return "participle";  
  if (x \=== "adverb") return "adverb";  
  if (x \=== "numeral") return "numeral";  
  if (x \=== "article") return "article";  
  if (x \=== "pronoun") return "pronoun";  
  if (x \=== "preposition") return "preposition";  
  if (x \=== "conjunction") return "conjunction";  
  if (x \=== "particle") return "particle";  
  if (x \=== "interjection") return "interjection";  
  return "unknown";  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* Minimal template parser (nesting safe)  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
export type TemplateCall \= {  
  raw: string;                    // "{{...}}"  
  name: string;                   // first token  
  positional: string\[\];           // unnamed args  
  named: Record<string, string\>;  // key=value args  
};  
  
export function extractTemplates(wikitext: string): TemplateCall\[\] {  
  const out: TemplateCall\[\] \= \[\];  
  let i \= 0;  
  
  while (i < wikitext.length) {  
    const start \= wikitext.indexOf("{{", i);  
    if (start < 0) break;  
  
    let depth \= 0;  
    let j \= start;  
  
    while (j < wikitext.length) {  
      if (wikitext.startsWith("{{", j)) {  
        depth++;  
        j += 2;  
        continue;  
      }  
      if (wikitext.startsWith("}}", j)) {  
        depth\--;  
        j += 2;  
        if (depth \=== 0) {  
          const raw \= wikitext.slice(start, j);  
          const call \= parseTemplateRaw(raw);  
          if (call) out.push(call);  
          break;  
        }  
        continue;  
      }  
      j++;  
    }  
  
    i \= Math.max(j, start + 2);  
  }  
  
  return out;  
}  
  
function parseTemplateRaw(raw: string): TemplateCall | null {  
  if (!raw.startsWith("{{") || !raw.endsWith("}}")) return null;  
  const inner \= raw.slice(2, \-2).trim();  
  if (!inner) return null;  
  
  const parts \= splitTopLevel(inner, "|");  
  const name \= (parts.shift() ?? "").trim();  
  if (!name) return null;  
  
  const positional: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  const named: Record<string, string\> \= {};  
  
  for (const p0 of parts) {  
    const p \= p0.trim();  
    const eq \= indexOfTopLevel(p, "=");  
    if (eq \> 0) {  
      const k \= p.slice(0, eq).trim();  
      const v \= p.slice(eq + 1).trim();  
      if (k) named\[k\] \= v;  
    } else {  
      positional.push(p);  
    }  
  }  
  
  return { raw, name, positional, named };  
}  
  
function splitTopLevel(s: string, delim: string): string\[\] {  
  const out: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  let buf \= "";  
  let depth \= 0;  
  
  for (let i \= 0; i < s.length; i++) {  
    if (s.startsWith("{{", i)) {  
      depth++; buf += "{{"; i++; continue;  
    }  
    if (s.startsWith("}}", i)) {  
      depth \= Math.max(0, depth \- 1); buf += "}}"; i++; continue;  
    }  
    if (depth \=== 0 && s.startsWith(delim, i)) {  
      out.push(buf); buf \= ""; continue;  
    }  
    buf += s\[i\];  
  }  
  out.push(buf);  
  return out;  
}  
  
function indexOfTopLevel(s: string, needle: string): number {  
  let depth \= 0;  
  for (let i \= 0; i < s.length; i++) {  
    if (s.startsWith("{{", i)) { depth++; i++; continue; }  
    if (s.startsWith("}}", i)) { depth \= Math.max(0, depth \- 1); i++; continue; }  
    if (depth \=== 0 && s.startsWith(needle, i)) return i;  
  }  
  return \-1;  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* Template decoders  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
function decodeHead(tpls: TemplateCall\[\], lang: string): { pos?: string; tags?: string\[\] } | undefined {  
  const head \= tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "head" && t.positional\[0\] \=== lang);  
  if (!head) return undefined;  
  const pos \= head.positional\[1\]?.trim();  
  const tags \= head.positional.slice(2).map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean);  
  return { pos: pos || undefined, tags: tags.length ? tags : undefined };  
}  
  
function parsePronunciationSection(wt: string, lang: WikiLang): Pronunciation | undefined {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  
  const ipaTpl \= tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "IPA" && (t.positional\[0\] \=== lang || t.named\["lang"\] \=== lang));  
  const hyphTpl \= tpls.find(t => (t.name \=== "hyphenation" || t.name \=== "hyph") && t.positional\[0\] \=== lang);  
  
  // optional audio patterns vary; keep minimal:  
  const audioTpl \=  
    tpls.find(t => (t.name \=== "audio" || t.name \=== "audio-IPA") && (t.positional\[0\] \=== lang || t.named\["lang"\] \=== lang))  
    ?? tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "audio" && t.positional.length \> 0);  
  
  const IPA \= ipaTpl?.positional?.find(x => x.startsWith("/") && x.endsWith("/"));  
  const hyphenation \= hyphTpl ? hyphTpl.positional.slice(1).join("‧") : undefined;  
  const audio \= audioTpl?.positional?.find(x => /\\.(ogg|oga|wav|mp3)$/i.test(x));  
  
  const out: Pronunciation \= {};  
  if (IPA) out.IPA \= IPA;  
  if (hyphenation) out.hyphenation \= hyphenation;  
  if (audio) out.audio \= audio;  
  
  return Object.keys(out).length ? out : undefined;  
}  
  
function findInflOf(tpls: TemplateCall\[\], lang: WikiLang): TemplateCall | undefined {  
  return tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "infl of" && t.positional\[0\] \=== lang);  
}  
  
function decodeInflOfTags(tags: string\[\]): {  
  verb?: {  
    person?: 1|2|3;  
    number?: "singular"|"plural";  
    tense?: "present"|"aorist"|"imperfect"|"future"|"unknown";  
    mood?: "indicative"|"subjunctive"|"imperative"|"unknown";  
    voice?: "active"|"middle"|"passive"|"unknown";  
  };  
  nominal?: {  
    case?: "nominative"|"genitive"|"accusative"|"vocative"|"unknown";  
    number?: "singular"|"plural";  
    gender?: "m"|"f"|"n"|"unknown";  
  };  
  raw: string\[\];  
} {  
  const raw \= tags.map(t => t.trim()).filter(Boolean);  
  
  const verb: any \= {};  
  const nominal: any \= {};  
  
  for (const t0 of raw) {  
    const t \= t0.toLowerCase();  
  
    // 1s,2p,3s...  
    const pn \= /^(\[123\])(\[sp\])$/.exec(t);  
    if (pn) {  
      verb.person \= Number(pn\[1\]) as 1|2|3;  
      verb.number \= pn\[2\] \=== "s" ? "singular" : "plural";  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // Verb tense/mood/voice  
    if (t \=== "spast") { verb.tense \= "aorist"; verb.mood \= "indicative"; verb.voice \= "active"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "pres")  { verb.tense \= "present"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "impf" || t \=== "imperfect") { verb.tense \= "imperfect"; verb.mood ??= "indicative"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "fut" || t \=== "future") { verb.tense \= "future"; continue; }  
    if (t \=== "ind") verb.mood \= "indicative";  
    if (t \=== "subj") verb.mood \= "subjunctive";  
    if (t \=== "imp") verb.mood \= "imperative";  
    if (t \=== "act") verb.voice \= "active";  
    if (t \=== "mid") verb.voice \= "middle";  
    if (t \=== "pass") verb.voice \= "passive";  
  
    // Nominal tags  
    if (t \=== "nom") nominal.case \= "nominative";  
    if (t \=== "gen") nominal.case \= "genitive";  
    if (t \=== "acc") nominal.case \= "accusative";  
    if (t \=== "voc") nominal.case \= "vocative";  
    if (t \=== "sg" || t \=== "s") nominal.number \= "singular";  
    if (t \=== "pl" || t \=== "p") nominal.number \= "plural";  
    if (t \=== "m" || t \=== "f" || t \=== "n") nominal.gender \= t;  
  }  
  
  const hasVerb \= Object.keys(verb).length \> 0;  
  const hasNom \= Object.keys(nominal).length \> 0;  
  
  if (hasVerb) {  
    verb.tense ??= "unknown";  
    verb.mood ??= "unknown";  
    verb.voice ??= "unknown";  
  }  
  if (hasNom) {  
    nominal.case ??= "unknown";  
    nominal.gender ??= "unknown";  
  }  
  
  return {  
    verb: hasVerb ? verb : undefined,  
    nominal: hasNom ? nominal : undefined,  
    raw,  
  };  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* Sense parsing: definitions + {{ux|...}} examples  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
function extractDefinitions(wt: string): string\[\] {  
  // Lines beginning with "# " are senses. Keep only top-level (# not ##).  
  const out: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  for (const line of wt.split(/\\r?\\n/)) {  
    const m \= /^\\s\*#\\s+(?!#)(.\*)\\s\*$/.exec(line);  
    if (!m) continue;  
    out.push(stripInlineWikitext(m\[1\]));  
  }  
  return out;  
}  
  
function extractUsageExamplesFromUx(wt: string, lang: WikiLang): UsageExample\[\] {  
  // {{ux|el|Greek sentence|t=English translation}}  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  const out: UsageExample\[\] \= \[\];  
  
  for (const t of tpls) {  
    if (t.name !== "ux") continue;  
    const l \= t.positional\[0\]?.trim();  
    if (l !== lang) continue;  
  
    const elSent \= t.positional\[1\] ? stripInlineWikitext(t.positional\[1\]) : undefined;  
    const en \= t.named\["t"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(t.named\["t"\]) : undefined;  
    const note \= t.named\["q"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(t.named\["q"\]) : undefined;  
  
    if (elSent || en) out.push({ el: elSent, en, note });  
  }  
  
  return out;  
}  
  
function stripInlineWikitext(s: string): string {  
  // Lightweight stripper: remove templates and simplify links.  
  // For production, you may later replace this with a proper wikitext AST.  
  let x \= s;  
  
  // Remove templates (non-greedy, best effort)  
  x \= x.replace(/\\{\\{\[^\]\*?\\}\\}/g, "");  
  
  // \[\[target|label\]\] -> label  
  x \= x.replace(/\\\[\\\[(\[^|\\\]\]+)\\|(\[^\\\]\]+)\\\]\\\]/g, "$2");  
  // \[\[target\]\] -> target  
  x \= x.replace(/\\\[\\\[(\[^\\\]\]+)\\\]\\\]/g, "$1");  
  
  // Bold/italic  
  x \= x.replace(/'''+/g, "");  
  x \= x.replace(/''+/g, "");  
  
  // Cleanup whitespace  
  x \= x.replace(/\\s+/g, " ").trim();  
  return x;  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* POS-specific mappers (expanded)  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
function inferVerbVoiceType(form: string): "active" | "mediopassive" | "unknown" {  
  if (form.endsWith("ομαι") || form.endsWith("μαι")) return "mediopassive";  
  if (form.endsWith("ω") || form.endsWith("ώ")) return "active";  
  return "unknown";  
}  
  
function inferVerbEnding(form: string): string | undefined {  
  if (form.endsWith("ομαι")) return "-ομαι";  
  if (form.endsWith("μαι")) return "-μαι";  
  if (form.endsWith("ω")) return "-ω";  
  if (form.endsWith("ώ")) return "-ώ";  
  if (form.endsWith("άω")) return "-άω";  
  return undefined;  
}  
  
function findGreekConjugationTemplate(tpls: TemplateCall\[\]): TemplateCall | undefined {  
  // el-conjug-1st, el-conjug-2nd, etc.  
  return tpls.find(t => t.name.startsWith("el-conjug-"));  
}  
  
function mapVerbLemma(  
  term: string,  
  lang: WikiLang,  
  etymology: string | undefined,  
  wt: string,  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation  
): VerbLexeme {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  const elVerb \= tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "el-verb");  
  const elConj \= findGreekConjugationTemplate(tpls);  
  
  const aorist1sg \= elVerb?.named\["past"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(elVerb.named\["past"\]) : undefined;  
  const passivePresent \= elVerb?.named\["passive"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(elVerb.named\["passive"\]) : undefined;  
  
  // Stems (best effort; template parameters vary across verb classes)  
  const presentStem \= elConj?.named\["present"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(elConj.named\["present"\]) : undefined;  
  const aDependent \= elConj?.named\["a-dependent"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(elConj.named\["a-dependent"\]) : undefined;  
  const aSimplePast \= elConj?.named\["a-simplepast"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(elConj.named\["a-simplepast"\]) : undefined;  
  const aImperfect \= elConj?.named\["a-imperfect"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(elConj.named\["a-imperfect"\]) : undefined;  
  const pSimplePast \= elConj?.named\["p-simplepast"\] ? stripInlineWikitext(elConj.named\["p-simplepast"\]) : undefined;  
  
  const augment \= elConj?.named\["augmented"\] \=== "1" ? "έ-" : undefined;  
  
  // crude passive aorist heuristic (works often for -τηκα patterns)  
  const passiveAorist \= pSimplePast ? \`${pSimplePast}ηκα\` : undefined;  
  
  const defs \= extractDefinitions(wt);  
  const usage \= extractUsageExamplesFromUx(wt, lang);  
  
  const senses \= defs.map((g, idx) => ({  
    gloss: g || undefined,  
    usage: usage.length ? usage : undefined,  
  }));  
  
  // derivations best-effort via {{l|el|...}}  
  const derivations \= extractLinkedTerms(tpls, lang);  
  
  const voiceType \= inferVerbVoiceType(term);  
  const ending \= inferVerbEnding(term);  
  
  // your “class” can later be refined; keep a stable heuristic now:  
  const cls \= voiceType \=== "active" && ending \=== "-ω" ? "verb.act.ω" : voiceType \=== "mediopassive" ? "verb.mp.ομαι" : undefined;  
  
  return {  
    id: mkEntryId(lang, term, etymology, "verb", "LEXEME"),  
    language: lang,  
    type: "LEXEME",  
    pos: "verb",  
    form: term,  
    etymology,  
    pronunciation,  
    class: cls,  
    voiceType,  
    morphology: {  
      presentStem: presentStem ? \`${presentStem}\-\` : undefined,  
      aoristStem: (aDependent || aSimplePast) ? \`${(aDependent ?? aSimplePast)!}\-\` : undefined,  
      augment,  
      ending,  
    },  
    paradigm: {  
      present\_1sg: term,  
      aorist\_1sg: aorist1sg,  
      imperfect\_3sg: aImperfect ? \`${aImperfect}ε\` : undefined,  
      passive\_present: passivePresent,  
      passive\_aorist: passiveAorist,  
    },  
    senses: senses.length ? senses : undefined,  
    derivations: derivations.length ? derivations : undefined,  
    \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, term, undefined, "Verb", tpls),  
  };  
}  
  
function mapVerbInflected(  
  term: string,  
  lang: WikiLang,  
  etymology: string | undefined,  
  wt: string,  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation  
): VerbInflected | null {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  const infl \= findInflOf(tpls, lang);  
  if (!infl) return null;  
  
  const lemmaForm \= stripInlineWikitext(infl.positional\[1\] ?? "").trim();  
  if (!lemmaForm) return null;  
  
  const tags \= infl.positional.slice(2).filter(Boolean);  
  const decoded \= decodeInflOfTags(tags);  
  
  return {  
    id: mkEntryId(lang, term, etymology, "verb", "INFLECTED\_FORM"),  
    language: lang,  
    type: "INFLECTED\_FORM",  
    pos: "verb",  
    form: term,  
    etymology,  
    pronunciation,  
    lemma: { id: mkEntryId(lang, lemmaForm, undefined, "verb", "LEXEME"), form: lemmaForm, pos: "verb" },  
    inflection: decoded.verb,  
    senses: sensesFromWikitext(lang, wt),  
    \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, term, undefined, "Verb", tpls),  
  };  
}  
  
function mapNounLemma(  
  term: string,  
  lang: WikiLang,  
  etymology: string | undefined,  
  wt: string,  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation  
): NounLexeme {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  const elNoun \= tpls.find(t => t.name \=== "el-noun");  
  
  // Gender params vary; start with common named ones:  
  const g \= (elNoun?.named\["g"\] ?? elNoun?.named\["g1"\] ?? "").trim().toLowerCase();  
  const gender: "m" | "f" | "n" | "unknown" \= g \=== "m" || g \=== "f" || g \=== "n" ? (g as any) : "unknown";  
  
  return {  
    id: mkEntryId(lang, term, etymology, "noun", "LEXEME"),  
    language: lang,  
    type: "LEXEME",  
    pos: "noun",  
    form: term,  
    etymology,  
    pronunciation,  
    gender,  
    senses: sensesFromWikitext(lang, wt),  
    \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, term, undefined, "Noun", tpls),  
  };  
}  
  
function mapNounInflected(  
  term: string,  
  lang: WikiLang,  
  etymology: string | undefined,  
  wt: string,  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation  
): NounInflected | null {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  const infl \= findInflOf(tpls, lang);  
  if (!infl) return null;  
  
  const lemmaForm \= stripInlineWikitext(infl.positional\[1\] ?? "").trim();  
  if (!lemmaForm) return null;  
  
  const tags \= infl.positional.slice(2).filter(Boolean);  
  const decoded \= decodeInflOfTags(tags);  
  
  return {  
    id: mkEntryId(lang, term, etymology, "noun", "INFLECTED\_FORM"),  
    language: lang,  
    type: "INFLECTED\_FORM",  
    pos: "noun",  
    form: term,  
    etymology,  
    pronunciation,  
    lemma: { id: mkEntryId(lang, lemmaForm, undefined, "noun", "LEXEME"), form: lemmaForm, pos: "noun" },  
    inflection: decoded.nominal,  
    senses: sensesFromWikitext(lang, wt),  
    \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, term, undefined, "Noun", tpls),  
  };  
}  
  
function mapAdjectiveLemma(  
  term: string,  
  lang: WikiLang,  
  etymology: string | undefined,  
  wt: string,  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation  
): AdjectiveLexeme {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  return {  
    id: mkEntryId(lang, term, etymology, "adjective", "LEXEME"),  
    language: lang,  
    type: "LEXEME",  
    pos: "adjective",  
    form: term,  
    etymology,  
    pronunciation,  
    senses: sensesFromWikitext(lang, wt),  
    \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, term, undefined, "Adjective", tpls),  
  };  
}  
  
function mapAdjectiveInflected(  
  term: string,  
  lang: WikiLang,  
  etymology: string | undefined,  
  wt: string,  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation,  
  pos: "adjective" | "participle"  
): AdjectiveInflected | null {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  const infl \= findInflOf(tpls, lang);  
  if (!infl) return null;  
  
  const lemmaForm \= stripInlineWikitext(infl.positional\[1\] ?? "").trim();  
  if (!lemmaForm) return null;  
  
  const tags \= infl.positional.slice(2).filter(Boolean);  
  const decoded \= decodeInflOfTags(tags);  
  
  return {  
    id: mkEntryId(lang, term, etymology, pos, "INFLECTED\_FORM"),  
    language: lang,  
    type: "INFLECTED\_FORM",  
    pos,  
    form: term,  
    etymology,  
    pronunciation,  
    lemma: { id: mkEntryId(lang, lemmaForm, undefined, pos, "LEXEME"), form: lemmaForm, pos },  
    inflection: decoded.nominal,  
    senses: sensesFromWikitext(lang, wt),  
    \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, term, undefined, pos \=== "participle" ? "Participle" : "Adjective", tpls),  
  };  
}  
  
function mapGenericLemma(  
  term: string,  
  lang: WikiLang,  
  etymology: string | undefined,  
  pos: Pos,  
  wt: string,  
  pronunciation?: Pronunciation  
): GenericLexeme {  
  const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
  return {  
    id: mkEntryId(lang, term, etymology, pos, "LEXEME"),  
    language: lang,  
    type: "LEXEME",  
    pos,  
    form: term,  
    etymology,  
    pronunciation,  
    senses: sensesFromWikitext(lang, wt),  
    \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, term, undefined, pos, tpls),  
  };  
}  
  
function sensesFromWikitext(lang: WikiLang, wt: string): BaseEntry\["senses"\] | undefined {  
  const defs \= extractDefinitions(wt);  
  const usage \= extractUsageExamplesFromUx(wt, lang);  
  if (!defs.length && !usage.length) return undefined;  
  
  // If no defs but examples exist, attach as one sense.  
  if (!defs.length && usage.length) return \[{ usage }\];  
  
  return defs.map(g => ({ gloss: g || undefined, usage: usage.length ? usage : undefined }));  
}  
  
function extractLinkedTerms(tpls: TemplateCall\[\], lang: WikiLang): string\[\] {  
  // {{l|el|TERM|...}} anywhere in this section  
  const out: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  const seen \= new Set<string\>();  
  for (const t of tpls) {  
    if (t.name !== "l") continue;  
    if ((t.positional\[0\] ?? "").trim() !== lang) continue;  
    const term \= stripInlineWikitext(t.positional\[1\] ?? "").trim();  
    if (!term) continue;  
    if (seen.has(term)) continue;  
    seen.add(term);  
    out.push(term);  
  }  
  return out;  
}  
  
function debugFromTemplates(  
  domain: string,  
  pageTitle: string,  
  sectionIndex: string | undefined,  
  sectionHeading: string,  
  tpls: TemplateCall\[\]  
): BaseEntry\["\_debug"\] {  
  const unknown \= collectUnknownTemplates(tpls);  
  return {  
    wiktionary: { domain, pageTitle, sectionIndex, sectionHeading },  
    templates: tpls.slice(0, 50).map(t => ({ name: t.name, raw: t.raw })), // cap  
    unknownTemplates: unknown.length ? unknown : undefined,  
  };  
}  
  
function collectUnknownTemplates(tpls: TemplateCall\[\]): string\[\] {  
  // A “coverage expansion” helper: flag templates we haven’t explicitly mapped.  
  // Keep it conservative (don’t mark universal ones).  
  const known \= new Set(\[  
    "infl of",  
    "el-verb",  
    "el-noun",  
    "el-adj",  
    "el-conjug-1st",  
    "el-conjug-2nd",  
    "el-conjug-",  
    "IPA",  
    "hyphenation",  
    "hyph",  
    "ux",  
    "l",  
    "head",  
    "audio",  
    "audio-IPA",  
  \]);  
  const out: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  const seen \= new Set<string\>();  
  
  for (const t of tpls) {  
    const n \= t.name;  
    const isKnown \=  
      known.has(n) ||  
      (n.startsWith("el-conjug-") && known.has("el-conjug-"));  
    if (!isKnown && !seen.has(n)) {  
      seen.add(n);  
      out.push(n);  
    }  
  }  
  return out;  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* ID policy + normalization  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
function mkEntryId(lang: WikiLang, form: string, etymology: string | undefined, pos: string, type: EntryType): string {  
  const et \= etymology ? \`#${etymology.replace(/\\s+/g, "")}\` : "";  
  // type doesn’t need to be in the id if pos+etymology already disambiguates, but keeping it helps debugging.  
  return \`${lang}:${form}${et}#${pos}#${type}\`;  
}  
  
function normalizeTerm(s: string): string {  
  return (s ?? "").trim().normalize("NFC");  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* Public API: fetchWiktionary(term)  
 \* ============================================================ \*/  
  
export async function fetchWiktionary(term: string, opts: Wiktionary SDKOptions \= {}): Promise<FetchResult\> {  
  const lang: WikiLang \= opts.lang ?? "el";  
  const timeoutMs \= opts.timeoutMs ?? 15\_000;  
  const followLemma \= opts.followLemma ?? true;  
  const includeLemmaEntry \= opts.includeLemmaEntry ?? true;  
  
  const warnings: string\[\] \= \[\];  
  const queryTerm \= normalizeTerm(term);  
  if (!queryTerm) {  
    return { query: { term, lang, posHint: opts.posHint }, entries: \[\], warnings: \["Empty query term."\] };  
  }  
  
  // 1) sections  
  const secResp \= await mwParseSections(queryTerm, timeoutMs);  
  if (secResp.error) {  
    return { query: { term: queryTerm, lang, posHint: opts.posHint }, entries: \[\], warnings: \[\`Wiktionary API error: ${secResp.error.code}: ${secResp.error.info}\`\] };  
  }  
  const sections \= (secResp.parse?.sections ?? \[\]).map(s => ({ index: s.index, line: s.line, level: Number(s.level) } satisfies MWSection));  
  const tree \= buildSectionTree(sections);  
  
  // 2) Greek node  
  const greekNode \= findLanguageNode(tree, "Greek");  
  if (!greekNode) {  
    return { query: { term: queryTerm, lang, posHint: opts.posHint }, entries: \[\], warnings: \["No ==Greek== section found on en.wiktionary page."\] };  
  }  
  
  const layout \= extractGreekLayout(greekNode);  
  
  // 3) pronunciation  
  let pronunciation: Pronunciation | undefined;  
  if (layout.pronunciationSection) {  
    const pr \= await mwParseWikitext(queryTerm, layout.pronunciationSection, timeoutMs);  
    if (!pr.error && pr.parse?.wikitext) {  
      pronunciation \= parsePronunciationSection(pr.parse.wikitext, lang);  
    }  
  }  
  
  // 4) decode each block (homonymy-aware)  
  const entries: Entry\[\] \= \[\];  
  const lemmaToFetch \= new Set<string\>();  
  
  for (const block of layout.blocks) {  
    const pos \= headingToPos(block.posHeading);  
    if (opts.posHint && pos !== opts.posHint) {  
      // still allow weak head-based override later; but keep simple filter:  
      // If user hints, skip unrelated pos headings.  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    const wtResp \= await mwParseWikitext(queryTerm, block.sectionIndex, timeoutMs);  
    if (wtResp.error || !wtResp.parse?.wikitext) continue;  
    const wt \= wtResp.parse.wikitext;  
  
    const tpls \= extractTemplates(wt);  
    const head \= decodeHead(tpls, lang);  
    const infl \= findInflOf(tpls, lang);  
  
    // POS override from head if it’s clearer  
    const headPos \= (head?.pos ?? "").trim().toLowerCase();  
    const headPosAsPos: Pos \=  
      headPos \=== "verb" ? "verb" :  
      headPos \=== "noun" ? "noun" :  
      headPos \=== "adjective" ? "adjective" :  
      headPos \=== "participle" ? "participle" :  
      headPos \=== "adverb" ? "adverb" :  
      headPos \=== "numeral" ? "numeral" :  
      headPos \=== "article" ? "article" :  
      headPos \=== "pronoun" ? "pronoun" :  
      headPos \=== "preposition" ? "preposition" :  
      headPos \=== "conjunction" ? "conjunction" :  
      headPos \=== "particle" ? "particle" :  
      headPos \=== "interjection" ? "interjection" :  
      headPos ? "function" : pos;  
  
    const effectivePos \= headPosAsPos !== "unknown" ? headPosAsPos : pos;  
  
    // INFLECTED\_FORM  
    if (infl) {  
      const lemmaForm \= stripInlineWikitext(infl.positional\[1\] ?? "").trim();  
      if (lemmaForm) lemmaToFetch.add(lemmaForm);  
  
      if (effectivePos \=== "verb") {  
        const e \= mapVerbInflected(queryTerm, lang, block.etymology, wt, pronunciation);  
        if (e) entries.push(e);  
        continue;  
      }  
      if (effectivePos \=== "noun") {  
        const e \= mapNounInflected(queryTerm, lang, block.etymology, wt, pronunciation);  
        if (e) entries.push(e);  
        continue;  
      }  
      if (effectivePos \=== "adjective" || effectivePos \=== "participle") {  
        const e \= mapAdjectiveInflected(queryTerm, lang, block.etymology, wt, pronunciation, effectivePos \=== "participle" ? "participle" : "adjective");  
        if (e) entries.push(e);  
        continue;  
      }  
  
      // Fallback: treat as function inflected  
      entries.push({  
        id: mkEntryId(lang, queryTerm, block.etymology, effectivePos, "INFLECTED\_FORM"),  
        language: lang,  
        type: "INFLECTED\_FORM",  
        pos: effectivePos,  
        form: queryTerm,  
        etymology: block.etymology,  
        pronunciation,  
        senses: sensesFromWikitext(lang, wt),  
        \_debug: debugFromTemplates(WIKTIONARY\_DOMAIN, queryTerm, block.sectionIndex, block.sectionHeading, tpls),  
      } as any);  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // LEXEME  
    if (effectivePos \=== "verb") {  
      entries.push(mapVerbLemma(queryTerm, lang, block.etymology, wt, pronunciation));  
      continue;  
    }  
    if (effectivePos \=== "noun") {  
      entries.push(mapNounLemma(queryTerm, lang, block.etymology, wt, pronunciation));  
      continue;  
    }  
    if (effectivePos \=== "adjective") {  
      entries.push(mapAdjectiveLemma(queryTerm, lang, block.etymology, wt, pronunciation));  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // numerals, particles, function words, etc.  
    entries.push(mapGenericLemma(queryTerm, lang, block.etymology, effectivePos, wt, pronunciation));  
  }  
  
  // 5) If query was inflected, fetch lemma entry/entries (lemma-centric strategy)  
  // We include lemma entries separately, so enrichment attaches naturally to lemma objects only.  
  if (followLemma && includeLemmaEntry && lemmaToFetch.size) {  
    for (const lemmaForm of lemmaToFetch) {  
      const lemmaRes \= await fetchWiktionary(lemmaForm, {  
        ...opts,  
        followLemma: false,  
        includeLemmaEntry: false,  
      });  
      // Keep only LEXEME entries from lemma fetch; avoid infinite expansions.  
      for (const e of lemmaRes.entries) {  
        if (e.type \=== "LEXEME") entries.push(e);  
      }  
    }  
  }  
  
  // 6) Lemma-only Wikidata enrichment  
  if (opts.enrich?.includeWikidata) {  
    const enriched: Entry\[\] \= \[\];  
    for (const e of entries) {  
      if (e.type !== "LEXEME") {  
        enriched.push(e);  
        continue;  
      }  
      const ee \= await enrichLemmaOnly(e, e.form, opts.enrich, timeoutMs);  
      enriched.push(ee);  
    }  
    return { query: { term: queryTerm, lang, posHint: opts.posHint }, entries: enriched, warnings };  
  }  
  
  if (!entries.length) warnings.push("No decodable entries found (current coverage depends on templates present in en.wiktionary).");  
  
  return { query: { term: queryTerm, lang, posHint: opts.posHint }, entries, warnings };  
}  
  
/\* ============================================================  
 \* Quick demo (optional)  
 \* ============================================================  
 \*  
 \* (async () => {  
 \*   const r1 = await fetchWiktionary("έγραψε", {  
 \*     lang: "el",  
 \*     followLemma: true,  
 \*     includeLemmaEntry: true,  
 \*     enrich: { includeWikidata: true, wikidataLanguages: \["en","el"\], imageWidth: 320 },  
 \*   });  
 \*   console.dir(r1, { depth: null });  
 \*  
 \*   const r2 = await fetchWiktionary("γράφω", {  
 \*     lang: "el",  
 \*     enrich: { includeWikidata: true, wikidataLanguages: \["en","el"\], imageWidth: 320 },  
 \*   });  
 \*   console.dir(r2, { depth: null });  
 \* })();  
 \*/
```

## What this implementation already gives you (concretely)

-   Query `έγραψε`:
    
    -   returns an **INFLECTED\_FORM** entry with:
        
        -   `lemma.form = "γράφω"`
            
        -   decoded `person/number/tense/mood/voice` (from `infl of` tags)
            
    -   **also returns** the lemma entry for `γράφω` (because `followLemma + includeLemmaEntry`)
        
    -   Wikidata enrichment attaches **only** to the lemma (`γράφω`) entry.
        
-   Query `spanakopita` (or any lemma that has a QID + P18):
    
    -   returns lemma lexicographic info from Wiktionary
        
    -   plus `wikidata.images[0].thumbUrl` suitable for your UI tile

# 1️⃣ Expanded `decodeInflOfTags` (Greek-aware)

We now support:

### Verb tags

-   1s / 2s / 3s / 1p / 2p / 3p
    
-   pres / impf / aor / spast / fut
    
-   ind / subj / imp
    
-   act / mid / pass
    
-   ptcp (participle)
    
-   mp (mediopassive shorthand)
    
-   perf (perfect)
    
-   nonfinite
    

### Nominal tags

-   nom / gen / acc / voc
    
-   sg / pl
    
-   m / f / n
    
-   dat (rare but present in older entries)
    

Replace your previous `decodeInflOfTags` with:

```
TypeScript

function decodeInflOfTags(tags: string\[\]): {  
  verb?: {  
    person?: 1|2|3;  
    number?: "singular"|"plural";  
    tense?: "present"|"aorist"|"imperfect"|"future"|"perfect"|"unknown";  
    mood?: "indicative"|"subjunctive"|"imperative"|"participle"|"nonfinite"|"unknown";  
    voice?: "active"|"middle"|"passive"|"mediopassive"|"unknown";  
  };  
  nominal?: {  
    case?: "nominative"|"genitive"|"accusative"|"vocative"|"dative"|"unknown";  
    number?: "singular"|"plural";  
    gender?: "m"|"f"|"n"|"unknown";  
  };  
  raw: string\[\];  
} {  
  const raw \= tags.map(t => t.trim()).filter(Boolean);  
  
  const verb: any \= {};  
  const nominal: any \= {};  
  
  for (const t0 of raw) {  
    const t \= t0.toLowerCase();  
  
    const pn \= /^(\[123\])(\[sp\])$/.exec(t);  
    if (pn) {  
      verb.person \= Number(pn\[1\]) as 1|2|3;  
      verb.number \= pn\[2\] \=== "s" ? "singular" : "plural";  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    // Tense  
    if (\["pres","present"\].includes(t)) verb.tense \= "present";  
    if (\["impf","imperfect"\].includes(t)) verb.tense \= "imperfect";  
    if (\["aor","spast"\].includes(t)) verb.tense \= "aorist";  
    if (\["fut","future"\].includes(t)) verb.tense \= "future";  
    if (\["perf","perfect"\].includes(t)) verb.tense \= "perfect";  
  
    // Mood  
    if (t \=== "ind") verb.mood \= "indicative";  
    if (t \=== "subj") verb.mood \= "subjunctive";  
    if (t \=== "imp") verb.mood \= "imperative";  
    if (t \=== "ptcp") verb.mood \= "participle";  
    if (t \=== "nonfinite") verb.mood \= "nonfinite";  
  
    // Voice  
    if (t \=== "act") verb.voice \= "active";  
    if (t \=== "mid") verb.voice \= "middle";  
    if (t \=== "pass") verb.voice \= "passive";  
    if (t \=== "mp") verb.voice \= "mediopassive";  
  
    // Nominal  
    if (t \=== "nom") nominal.case \= "nominative";  
    if (t \=== "gen") nominal.case \= "genitive";  
    if (t \=== "acc") nominal.case \= "accusative";  
    if (t \=== "voc") nominal.case \= "vocative";  
    if (t \=== "dat") nominal.case \= "dative";  
    if (\["sg","s"\].includes(t)) nominal.number \= "singular";  
    if (\["pl","p"\].includes(t)) nominal.number \= "plural";  
    if (\["m","f","n"\].includes(t)) nominal.gender \= t;  
  }  
  
  if (Object.keys(verb).length) {  
    verb.tense ??= "unknown";  
    verb.mood ??= "unknown";  
    verb.voice ??= "unknown";  
  }  
  
  if (Object.keys(nominal).length) {  
    nominal.case ??= "unknown";  
    nominal.gender ??= "unknown";  
  }  
  
  return {  
    verb: Object.keys(verb).length ? verb : undefined,  
    nominal: Object.keys(nominal).length ? nominal : undefined,  
    raw,  
  };  
}
```

This dramatically improves real Greek inflected-form resolution.

# 2️⃣ Explicit Translations Section Parser

English Wiktionary uses a block like:

```
Code

\====Translations====  
{{trans-top|to write}}  
\* English: {{t|en|write}}  
\* French: {{t|fr|écrire}}  
{{trans-bottom}}
```

We will now explicitly parse that.

Add:

```
TypeScript

function extractTranslations(wt: string): Record<string, string\[\]> | undefined {  
  const lines \= wt.split(/\\r?\\n/);  
  const out: Record<string, string\[\]> \= {};  
  let inTranslations \= false;  
  
  for (const line of lines) {  
    if (/^=+\\s\*Translations\\s\*=+/.test(line)) {  
      inTranslations \= true;  
      continue;  
    }  
  
    if (inTranslations && /^=+/.test(line)) {  
      // next section  
      break;  
    }  
  
    if (!inTranslations) continue;  
  
    // Lines like: \* English: {{t|en|write}}  
    const langMatch \= /^\\\*\\s\*(\[^:\]+):\\s\*(.\*)$/.exec(line);  
    if (!langMatch) continue;  
  
    const langLabel \= langMatch\[1\].trim();  
    const rest \= langMatch\[2\];  
  
    const tpls \= extractTemplates(rest);  
    for (const t of tpls) {  
      if (t.name \=== "t" || t.name \=== "t+" || t.name \=== "t-simple") {  
        const gloss \= stripInlineWikitext(t.positional\[1\] ?? "");  
        if (!gloss) continue;  
        if (!out\[langLabel\]) out\[langLabel\] \= \[\];  
        out\[langLabel\].push(gloss);  
      }  
    }  
  }  
  
  return Object.keys(out).length ? out : undefined;  
}
```

Now in each lemma mapper, add:

```
TypeScript

const translations \= extractTranslations(wt);
```

and include in returned entry:

```
TypeScript

translations,
```

This now gives you a structured `translations` object.

---

# 3️⃣ Preferred Lemma PoS Resolution

Problem:

If lemma has:

-   noun
    
-   verb
    

and we fetched lemma because an inflected verb form referenced it, we must choose the **verb** lemma.

### Solution:

When fetching lemma entries, filter by the PoS of the inflected entry.

Modify this block in `fetchWiktionary`:

Replace:

```
TypeScript

for (const e of lemmaRes.entries) {  
  if (e.type \=== "LEXEME") entries.push(e);  
}
```

With:

```
TypeScript

for (const inflEntry of entries.filter(e => e.type \=== "INFLECTED\_FORM")) {  
  const targetPos \= inflEntry.pos;  
  
  const lemmaCandidates \= lemmaRes.entries.filter(  
    e => e.type \=== "LEXEME" && e.pos \=== targetPos  
  );  
  
  if (lemmaCandidates.length) {  
    entries.push(...lemmaCandidates);  
  } else {  
    // fallback if no matching PoS found  
    entries.push(...lemmaRes.entries.filter(e => e.type \=== "LEXEME"));  
  }  
}
```

This ensures:

-   έγραψε → γράφω (verb only)
    
-   του σπιτιού → σπίτι (noun only)
    

Homonymy resolution is now **morphology-driven**, not arbitrary.
